Supplementary file S2  Alignments of conotoxin precursors, hormones, and other venom-related proteins derived 
from the Virroconus ebraeus and Virroconus judeus transcriptomes with homologues from closely-related cone snail species from West Africa (codes V_ and A_; Abalde et al, 2020) and 
Lautoconus ventricosus (code CV8; Pardos-Blas et al 2021) and from other cone species available in GenBank (the accession number follows the species name).
